FINAL("WITH annual AS (
  SELECT c.Segment,
         c.CustomerID,
         SUM(y.Consumption) AS annual_consumption
  FROM yearmonth AS y
  INNER JOIN customers AS c
    ON y.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
    AND y.Date BETWEEN '201301' AND '201312'
  GROUP BY c.Segment, c.CustomerID
),
min_segment AS (
  SELECT Segment,
         MIN(annual_consumption) AS min_annual_consumption
  FROM annual
  GROUP BY Segment
),
segment_avg AS (
  SELECT a.Segment,
         AVG(a.annual_consumption) AS avg_annual_consumption
  FROM annual AS a
  INNER JOIN min_segment AS m
    ON a.Segment = m.Segment
   AND a.annual_consumption = m.min_annual_consumption
  GROUP BY a.Segment
)
SELECT
  (SELECT avg_annual_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'SME')
  - (SELECT avg_annual_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'LAM') AS SME_LAM,
  (SELECT avg_annual_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'LAM')
  - (SELECT avg_annual_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'KAM') AS LAM_KAM,
  (SELECT avg_annual_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'KAM')
  - (SELECT avg_annual_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'SME') AS KAM_SME;")

FINAL("WITH annual AS (
  SELECT c.Segment,
         c.CustomerID,
         SUM(y.Consumption) AS annual_consumption
  FROM yearmonth AS y
  JOIN customers AS c
    ON y.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'CZK'
    AND y.Date BETWEEN '201301' AND '201312'
  GROUP BY c.Segment, c.CustomerID
),
min_consumption AS (
  SELECT Segment,
         MIN(annual_consumption) AS min_consumption
  FROM annual
  GROUP BY Segment
),
lowest_customers AS (
  SELECT a.Segment,
         a.CustomerID,
         a.annual_consumption
  FROM annual AS a
  JOIN min_consumption AS m
    ON a.Segment = m.Segment
   AND a.annual_consumption = m.min_consumption
),
segment_avg AS (
  SELECT Segment,
         SUM(annual_consumption) * 1.0 / COUNT(*) AS avg_consumption
  FROM lowest_customers
  GROUP BY Segment
)
SELECT
  (SELECT avg_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'SME')
  - (SELECT avg_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'LAM') AS SME_LAM,
  (SELECT avg_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'LAM')
  - (SELECT avg_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'KAM') AS LAM_KAM,
  (SELECT avg_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'KAM')
  - (SELECT avg_consumption FROM segment_avg WHERE Segment = 'SME') AS KAM_SME;")

```python
db.execute("""
```
```python
WITH seg AS (
  SELECT
    c.Segment,
    SUM(CASE WHEN substr(y.Date,1,4) = '2012' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END) AS cons2012,
    SUM(CASE WHEN substr(y.Date,1,4) = '2013' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END) AS cons2013
  FROM yearmonth y
  JOIN customers c ON y.CustomerID = c.CustomerID
  WHERE c.Currency = 'EUR'
    AND c.Segment IN ('SME', 'LAM', 'KAM')
  GROUP BY c.Segment
)
SELECT
  Segment,
  cons2012,
  cons2013,
  (cons2013 - cons2012) AS increase,
  ((cons2013 - cons2012) * 100.0 / cons2013) AS pct_increase
FROM seg
ORDER BY pct_increase DESC;
""")
```

SIMILAR SOLVED EXAMPLES (different databases — copy the SQL *style* and output-column conventions, not the table names):

  Q: What is the percentage of the most common conditions for patients age 60 and above?
  Hint: most common condition refers to MAX(COUNT(conditions.DESCRIPTION)); age 60 and above refers to SUBTRACT(conditions.START, birthdate) > 60; percentage = MULTIPLY(DIVIDE(SUM(patients.patient WHERE MAX(COUNT(conditions.DESCRIPTION)) AND SUBTRACT(conditions.START, birthdate) > 60))), COUNT(patients.patient WHERE MAX(COUNT(conditions.DESCRIPTION)), 10);
  SQL: SELECT CAST(SUM(CASE WHEN T5.DESCRIPTION = T3.DESCRIPTION THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS REAL) * 100 / COUNT(T3.patient) FROM ( SELECT T2.DESCRIPTION, T1.patient FROM patients AS T1 INNER JOIN conditions AS T2 ON T1.patient = T2.PATIENT WHERE ROUND((strftime('%J', T2.START) - strftime('%J', T1.birthdate)) / 365) > 60 GROUP BY T2.DESCRIPTION ORDER BY COUNT(T2.DESCRIPTION) DESC LIMIT 1 ) AS T3 INNER JOIN patients AS T4 ON T3.patient = T4.patient INNER JOIN conditions AS T5 ON T4.patient = T5.PATIENT WHERE ROUND((strftime('%J', T5.START) - strftime('%J', T4.birthdate)) / 365) > 60

  - Segment (TEXT); meaning=chain segment; examples=Value for money, Premium
- TABLE products; rows=591:

🤖 model turn:

I'll inspect the transaction date format and find the matching customer, then compute the 2012→2013 consumption decrease rate.
```python
db.sample_values("transactions_1k", "Date")
```
SELECT
  (SUM(CASE WHEN y.Date LIKE '2012%' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END) - SUM(CASE WHEN y.Date LIKE '2013%' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END))
  / NULLIF(SUM(CASE WHEN y.Date LIKE '2012%' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END), 0) AS consumption_decrease_rate
FROM yearmonth AS y
WHERE y.CustomerID = (
  SELECT t.CustomerID
  FROM transactions_1k AS t
  WHERE STRFTIME('%Y-%m-%d', t.Date) = '2012-08-25'
    AND ROUND(t.Amount * t.Price, 1) = 634.8
  ORDER BY t.TransactionID
  LIMIT 1
);

FINAL("WITH target_customer AS (SELECT DISTINCT CustomerID FROM transactions_1k WHERE Date = '2012-08-25' AND ABS(Amount * Price - 634.8) < 0.001 ORDER BY CustomerID LIMIT 1), annual AS (SELECT y.CustomerID, SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(y.Date,1,4) = '2012' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2012, SUM(CASE WHEN SUBSTR(y.Date,1,4) = '2013' THEN y.Consumption ELSE 0 END) AS consumption_2013 FROM yearmonth AS y JOIN target_customer AS tc ON y.CustomerID = tc.CustomerID WHERE SUBSTR(y.Date,1,4) IN ('2012', '2013') GROUP BY y.CustomerID) SELECT (consumption_2012 - consumption_2013) / NULLIF(consumption_2012, 0) AS consumption_decrease_rate FROM annual;")
